###########################
# USA Events By herkles
###########################

add_namespace = ustates
add_namespace = nimatron

country_event = { # Start up Event
	id = ustates.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1"}
	title = ustates.1.t
	desc = ustates.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_start_economic_timer
			set_country_flag = { flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power value = 5 }
			set_country_flag = { flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power value = 5 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.27
				days = 8
			} #Criminals
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.29
				days = 20
			} #ODP Bids
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.1200
				days = 50
			} #ODP Bids
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Chapin Death
	id = ustates.1200
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1200"}
	title = ustates.1200.t
	desc = ustates.1200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.1200.a
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.03
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = Roy_Dikeman_Chapin_Sr_dead
		}
		if = {
		limit = { has_idea = USA_Roy_Dikeman_Chapin_Sr_eco_mli }
		remove_ideas = USA_Roy_Dikeman_Chapin_Sr_eco_mli
		add_ideas = USA_Ray_Lyman_Wilbur_Sr_eco_mli
		}
	}
}

		add_stability = -0.03

	}
}

country_event = { # The Coalition Ticket?
	id = ustates.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3"}
	title = ustates.3.t
	desc = ustates.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		date > 1936.2.05
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
			has_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
			has_country_flag = USA_considered_coalition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = USA_considered_coalition
	}

	option = { # Form the Coalition
		name = ustates.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = 3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.3001
				days = 20
				} #GOP Candidate
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.4
				days = 180
				} #GOP Candidate
		}
	}
	option = { # Don't form the coalition
		name = ustates.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TXS_independence
					option = TXS_INDEPENDENCE_GUARENTEE
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.3001
				days = 20
				} #GOP Candidate
		}
	}
}


### Coalition stuff

country_event = { # Republican Nomination
	id = ustates.3001
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3001" }
	title = ustates.3001.t
	desc = ustates.3001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Curtis
		name = ustates.3001.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_rep_nomination
					option = USA_REP_NOM_LANDON
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.01 }
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = USA_curtis_nominated
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.5
				days = 35
			} #Dem Nomination
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.6
				days = 75
			} #Speech
		}
	}
	option = { # Landon
		name = ustates.3001.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_rep_nomination
						option = USA_REP_NOM_CURTIS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_rep_nomination
						option = USA_REP_NOM_HOOVER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.02 }
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = USA_landon_nominated
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.5
				days = 35
			} #Dem Nomination
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.6001
				days = 75
			} #Speech
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Curtis's Health in question
	id = ustates.4001
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.4001" }
	title = ustates.4001.t
	desc = ustates.4001.d
	picture = GFX_USA_curtis_nervous

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		date > 1936.3.10
		has_country_flag = USA_curtis_nominated
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = USA_gwbill_passes
			has_country_flag = USA_gwbill_notpasses
		}
	}
	option = { # Landon
		name = ustates.4001.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_rep_nomination
						option = USA_REP_NOM_CURTIS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_rep_nomination
						option = USA_REP_NOM_HOOVER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.02 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_landon_nominated
			clr_country_flag = USA_curtis_nominated
			country_event = { id = ustates.6000 days = 70 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep Curtis
		name = ustates.4001.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_rep_nomination
					option = USA_REP_NOM_HOOVER
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.01 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_curtis_nominated
			country_event = { id = ustates.6 days = 70 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Bring in Hoover
		name = ustates.4001.c
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_gwbill_passes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_rep_nomination
					option = USA_REP_NOM_CURTIS
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.01 }
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_hoover_nominated
			clr_country_flag = USA_curtis_nominated
			country_event = { id = ustates.3999 days = 70 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Fighting in Indiana
	id = ustates.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.7"}
	title = ustates.7.t
	desc = ustates.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Fight Both
		name = ustates.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -65
		add_manpower = -1150
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_ODP_loses_strength
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_loses_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = -1 }
			add_to_variable = { var = ODP_strength value = -1 }
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
	option = { # Fight the Klan
		name = ustates.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_manpower = -600
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_ODP_loses_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = ODP_strength value = -1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Fight the Socialists
		name = ustates.7.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_manpower = -450
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_loses_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = -1 }
		}
		}
	option = { # Fight Neither
		name = ustates.7.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_ODP_gains_strength
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { var = ODP_strength value = 1 }
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = { # Father Charles Coughlin's CBS Radio Broadcasts
	id = ustates.18
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.18"}
	title = ustates.18.t
	desc = ustates.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_father_coughlin

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by a papal event

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ustates.18.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PAP
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PAP
				modifier = COUGHLIN_RADIO_STOP
			} # 20
		}
		else = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ITA
				modifier = COUGHLIN_RADIO_STOP
			} # 20
		}
		add_political_power = -80
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
			} # they are more energized by shutting him down
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
			} # they are more energized by shutting him down
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
				id = ustates.19
				days = 15
			} #Huey
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.18.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PAP
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PAP
				modifier = COUGHLIN_RADIO_CONTINUES
			} # -15
		}
		else = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ITA
				modifier = COUGHLIN_RADIO_CONTINUES
			} # -15
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
			} # not as energized
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
			} # not as energized
			hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
				id = ustates.19
				days = 20
			} #Huey
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The great Migration
	id = ustates.134
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.134"}
	title = ustates.134.t
	desc = ustates.134.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_reconstruction

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag
		OR = {
			country_exists = CAL
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				has_democratic_government = yes
				any_owned_state = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CAL
			}
			CAL = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NEE
			}
			NEE = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAN = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # kill them
		name = ustates.134.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration1
			days = 90
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_stability = 0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.135
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Let them go
		name = ustates.134.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_war_support = -0.02
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration2
			days = 50
		}
		add_manpower = -2500
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.135
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Upcoming Election
	id = ustates.190
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.190"}
	title = ustates.190.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.190.d.progs
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.190.d.landon
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.190.d.curtis
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.190.d.garner
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Deadlock Garner Presidency
		text = ustates.190.d.deadlockgarner
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
		}
	}
	desc = { # Deadlock Norris Presidency
		text = ustates.190.d.deadlocknorris
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Interesting...
		name = ustates.190.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = { #PP-S
					ideology = syndicalist
					long_name = PP_syndicalist_coalition_long
					name = PP_syndicalist_coalition
				}
				set_party_name = { #PP-P
					ideology = social_democrat
					long_name = PP_social_democrat_coalition_long
					name = PP_social_democrat_coalition
				}
			}
		}
		
	option = { # Interesting...
		name = ustates.190.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = { #NPP-M-M
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = NPP_authoritarian_democrat_coalition_long
					name = NPP_authoritarian_democrat_coalition
				}
				set_party_name = { #NPP-F
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = NPP_paternal_autocrat_coalition_long
					name = NPP_paternal_autocrat_coalition
				}
				set_party_name = { #NPP-K
					ideology = national_populist
					long_name = NPP_national_populist_coalition_long
					name = NPP_national_populist_coalition
				}
				create_country_leader = { 
					name = "William H. Murray"
					desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_H_MURRAY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/COR/Portrait_William_H_Murray_2.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
					traits = { alfalfa_bill }
				}
				create_country_leader = { 
					name = "Charles Lindbergh"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_LINDBERGH"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/COR/COR_lindberg.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = jacksonianism_subtype
					traits = { the_lone_eagle }
				}
			}
		}

	option = { # Interesting...
		name = ustates.190.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
			OR = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		}
	}

country_event = { # The San Fran Conference
	id = ustates.191
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.191"}
	title = ustates.191.t
	desc = { # Sinclair
		text = ustates.191.d.sinclair
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
			}
		}
	desc = { # Hearst
		text = ustates.191.d.hearst
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
			}
		}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Success
		name = ustates.191.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PP_gains_strength
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Sinclair_endorses_PP
			set_party_name = { #PP-L
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = PP_radical_socialist_coalition_long
				name = PP_radical_socialist_coalition
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Failure
		name = ustates.191.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PP_loses_strength
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = -0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = Sinclair_does_not_endorse_PP
		}
	}
	option = { # Success
		name = ustates.191.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NPP_gains_strength
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = Hearst_endorses_NPP
		}
	}
	option = { # Failure
		name = ustates.191.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NPP_loses_strength
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = Hearst_does_not_endorse_NPP
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The St. Louis Convention, Presidential Nominee
	id = ustates.198
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.198"}
	title = ustates.198.t
	desc = { # Populist Party
		text = ustates.198.d.pp
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
			}
		}
	desc = { # National People's Party
		text = ustates.198.d.npp
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
			}
		}
	picture = GFX_event_kiel_auditorium
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # PP Party Nominee
		name = ustates.198.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
			NOT = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = reed_PP_strength
				compare = equals
				value = long_PP_strength
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Long
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = long_PP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ustates.1981 days = 1 }
			}
			if = { # Reed
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = reed_PP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ustates.1982 days = 1 }
			}
			if = { # deadlock
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = reed_PP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = long_PP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ustates.199 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # NPP Party Nominee
		name = ustates.198.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
			NOT = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = murray_NPP_strength
				compare = equals
				value = lindbergh_NPP_strength
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Murray
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = murray_NPP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ustates.1983 days = 1 }
			}
			if = { # Lindbergh
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = lindbergh_NPP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ustates.1984 days = 1 }
			}
			if = { # deadlock
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = murray_NPP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = lindbergh_NPP_strength
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ustates.199 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # the the lazy dead lock option
		name = ustates.198.c
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.199 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

					has_country_flag = Aiken_does_not_endorse_PP
					has_country_flag = Norris_does_not_endorse_PP
					has_country_flag = Sinclair_endorses_PP
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = ustates.1991 days = 1 }
	}
	option = { # PP Unity Candidate
		name = ustates.199.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner

					has_country_flag = browder_PP_convention_speaker

					has_country_flag = Sinclair_endorses_PP

				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.201.d.presidency
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Alf Landon"
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Charles Curtis"
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Herbert Hoover"
				}
			}
		}
	}

			has_country_leader = {

			}
			has_country_flag = USA_More_terms_for_herb
		}

			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes

			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_More_terms_for_herb }
		}

		NOT  = {

		}
		NOT  = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}

	}

				}

		}

		}

					name = "Charles Curtis"

					}

				set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_NPP_graves
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.204
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.205
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
}

### 1944 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # Choosing the PP Candidate
	id = ustates.1995
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1995"}
	title = ustates.1995.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	desc = { # Presidency
		text = ustates.1995.desc.presidency
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_huey
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_reed
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_maloney
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_sinclair
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_thomas
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_browder
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # No Presidency
		text = ustates.1995.d.nopresidency
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Re-Nominate PP Candidate
		name = ustates.1995.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_soc_dem_PP
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_rad_soc_PP
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_huey
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_huey
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_reed
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_reed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_maloney
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_maloney
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_sinclair
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_sinclair
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_thomas
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_thomas
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_browder
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_browder
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Earl Browder
		name = ustates.1995.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_browder
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Earl Browder"
				desc = "POLITICS_EARL_BROWDER_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Earl_Bowder.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = ustates.1995.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_sinclair
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Upton Sinclair"
				desc = "POLITICS_UPTON_SINCLAIR_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Upton_Sinclair.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				traits = { author }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Earl Long
		name = ustates.1995.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_earl
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Earl Long"
				desc = "POLITICS_EARL_LONG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TEX/Portrait_TEX_Earl_Kemp_Long.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = socdem_longism_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Robert M. La Follette Jr.
		name = ustates.1995.f
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_PP_primary_bob
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = " Robert M. La Follette Jr."
				desc = "POLITICS_ROBERT_FOLLETTE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TEX/Portrait_TEX_Bob_La_Follette_JR.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = centrist_subtype
				traits = { spirit_of_fighting_bob PSA_legacy_of_progressivism }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.204
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.204"}
	title = ustates.204.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	desc = { # Progressive Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.204.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.204.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # NPP Rivals, Kept Name
		text = ustates.204.d.NPP_rival_kept_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # NPP Rivals, New Name
		text = ustates.204.d.NPP_rival_new_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_new_name
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # Progressive Party has the Presidency-NPP Rivals, Kept Name
		text = ustates.204.d.president_npp_rivals_kept_name
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # Progressive Party has the Presidency-NPP Rivals, Kept Name
		text = ustates.204.d.president_npp_rivals_new_name
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		}
		NOT  = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = ustates.204.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_wallace
		}
	}
	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.204.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette
		}
	}
	option = { # Alfred Mitchell Bingham
		name = ustates.204.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_bingham
		}
	}
	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = ustates.204.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_sinclair
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Republican Primary
	id = ustates.205
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.205"}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	desc = { # Republican Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.205.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.205.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
			NOT  = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_garner
			}
			NOT  = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_PP_dominance
		}
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # nominate Thomas Dewey
		name = ustates.205.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
		}
	}
	option = { # nominate Quentin Roosevelt
		name = ustates.205.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_roosevelt
		}
	}
	option = { # Re-nominate the President
		name = ustates.205.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.206
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.206"}
	title = ustates.206.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	desc = { # Democratic Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.206.d.president
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.206.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_PP_dominance
		}
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		}
		NOT  = {
			has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Alben W. Barkley
		name = ustates.206.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # James E. Murray
		name = ustates.206.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # re-nominate the President
		name = ustates.206.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Wendell Willkie"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				modify_country_flag = {
					flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
					value = -1
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				modify_country_flag = {
					flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry F. Byrd"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				modify_country_flag = {
					flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
					value = 1
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				modify_country_flag = {
					flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Douglas MacArthur"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				modify_country_flag = {
					flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
					value = 1
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				modify_country_flag = {
					flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Election
	id = ustates.207
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.207"}
	title = ustates.207.t
	desc = ustates.207.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_PP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Philip La Follette"
					desc = "POLITICS_PHILIP_FOLLETTE_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Philip_La_Follette.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = georgism_subtype
					traits = { reluctant_interventionist }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_wallace
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry Wallace"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = georgism_subtype
					traits = { great_survivor }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_bingham
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Alfred Mitchell Bingham"
					desc = "POLITICS_ALFRED_MITCHELL_BINGHAM_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TEX/TEX_Alfred_Bingham.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
					traits = { educator }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_sinclair
					}

				set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_NPP_thurmond
			}
			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
}

### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # Choosing the PP Candidate
	id = ustates.1997
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1997"}
	title = ustates.1997.t
	desc = { # President, two terms
		text = ustates.1997.d.president_two_terms
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_huey
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_reed
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_maloney
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_folsom
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_thomas
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # President, one term
		text = ustates.1997.d.president_one_term
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_earl
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_browder
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_sinclair
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_bob
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Browder's Third Term
		text = ustates.1997.d.president_browder_third_term
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_browder
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_browder
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # No Presidency
		text = ustates.1997.d.nopresidency
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Re-Nominate PP Candidate
		name = ustates.1997.a
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_browder
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_sinclair
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_earl
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_bob
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_soc_dem_PP
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_rad_soc_PP
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_sinclair
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_sinclair
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_earl
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_earl
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_bob
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_bob
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_browder
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_browder
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Earl Browder
		name = ustates.1997.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_browder
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Earl Browder"
				desc = "POLITICS_EARL_BROWDER_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Earl_Bowder.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Sam DeWitt
		name = ustates.1997.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_dewitt
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Sam DeWitt"
				desc = "POLITICS_SAM_DEWITT_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Sam_DeWitt.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				traits = { author }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = ustates.1997.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_wallace
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Henry Wallace"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLACE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = georgism_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Philip LaFollette
		name = ustates.1997.f
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_philip
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Philip La Follette"
				desc = "POLITICS_PHILIP_FOLLETTE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Philip_La_Follette.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = georgism_subtype
				traits = { spirit_of_fighting_bob }
			}

country_event = { # 1948 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.209
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.209"}
	title = ustates.209.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.209.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.209.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.209.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # NPP Rivals, Kept Name

		trigger = {

		}
	}

			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_new_name

	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time-NPP Rivals, New Name

		trigger = {

			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance

			NOT = {

		}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance

		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			OR = {

				}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.211"}

	title = { # Liberal democrats founded their own party
		text = ustates.211.t.liberals
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats
		}
	}
	title = { # Conservative democrats founded their own party
		text = ustates.211.t.conservative
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_market_liberals_democrats
		}
	}

	desc = { # democrats Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.211.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}
	}

	desc = { # democrats Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.211.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # democrats Party does not have the Presidency - conservatives split off
		text = ustates.211.d.not_president_conservative
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # democrats Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.211.d.not_president_liberal
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			has_country_flag = USA_social_conservatives_democrats
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_PP_dominance
		}
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		}
		NOT  = {
				has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Harry Truman
		name = ustates.211.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = market_liberal
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
				}
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_truman
		}
	}
	option = { # William Averell Harriman
		name = ustates.211.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = market_liberal
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
				}
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_harriman
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = ustates.211.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_president
		}
	}
}

		}

	desc = { # Democrat Party won the presidency just last time

			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democrat Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.212.d.president_steps_down

			has_government = social_conservative
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat

			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_market_liberals_democrats
			}
		}
	}

		text = ustates.212.d.not_president_conservative
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative

		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		}
		NOT  = {
				has_country_flag = USA_deadlock_norris
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Strom Thurmond
		name = ustates.212.a

			OR = {

				}

					has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
				}
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
				has_country_flag = USA_civil_war_avoided_flag
			}
		}

		}
	}
	option = { # Happy Chandler

				}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_PP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance

### 1952 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # Choosing the PP Candidate
	id = ustates.1999
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1999"}
	title = ustates.1999.t
	desc = { # President, two terms
		text = ustates.1999.d.president_two_terms
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_sinclair
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_bob
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_browder
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_earl
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # President, one term
		text = ustates.1999.d.president_one_term
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_philip
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_dewitt
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_wallace
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Browder's Third Term
		text = ustates.1999.d.president_browder_third_term
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_browder
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_browder
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Browder's Fourth Term
		text = ustates.1999.d.president_browder_fourth_term
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_PP_browder
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_PP_browder
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_browder
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # No Presidency
		text = ustates.1999.d.nopresidency
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Re-Nominate PP Candidate
		name = ustates.1999.a
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
					has_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_dewitt
					has_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_philip
					has_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_wallace
					has_country_flag = USA_1948_PP_primary_browder
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_soc_dem_PP
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_rad_soc_PP
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_browder
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_browder
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_wallace
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_wallace
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_dewitt
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_dewitt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_PP_philip
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_philip
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Gus Hall
		name = ustates.1999.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_hall
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Gus Hall"
				desc = "POLITICS_GUS_HALL_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Gus_Hall.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Darlington Hoopes
		name = ustates.1999.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_hoopes
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Darlington Hoopes"
				desc = "POLITICS_DARLINGTON_HOOPES_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Darlington_Hoopes.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = ustates.1999.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_PP_primary_taylor
			create_country_leader = {

	id = ustates.214
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.214"}
	title = ustates.214.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.214.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1944
		text = ustates.214.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency-Soc Dem
		text = ustates.214.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
        text = ustates.214.d.not_president_reagan
        trigger = {
            NOT = {
                has_government = social_democrat
                has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_avoided_flag
                has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_avoided_flag
            }
            has_country_flag = USA_Radio_Reagan
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = USA_NORRIS_PRES
            }
        }
    }
	
	desc = { # NPP Rivals, Kept Name
		text = ustates.214.d.NPP_rival_kept_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # NPP Rivals, New Name
		text = ustates.214.d.NPP_rival_new_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_new_name
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time-NPP Rivals, Kept Name
		text = ustates.214.d.president_npp_rivals_kept_name

			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive

		}
	}
	
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1944-NPP Rivals, Kept Name
		text = ustates.214.d.president_steps_down_npp_rivals_kept_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
		}
	}
	
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time-NPP Rivals, New Name
		text = ustates.214.d.president_npp_rivals_new_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			NOT = {

			}
		}
	}

		text = ustates.214.d.president_steps_down_npp_rivals_new_name
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_rival_kept_name
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.214.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
				}
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_folette
		}
	}
	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = ustates.214.b
		trigger = {

				}
				NOT = {

		}
		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}
	option = { # Bingham

			}
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_PP_dominance
			has_country_flag = USA_NPP_dominance
		}

### League of American States  ###
country_event = { # Join the League?
	id = ustates.250
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.250"}
	title = ustates.250.t
	desc = ustates.250.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.250.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				tag = YUC
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.85
				OR = {
					tag = MEX
					tag = CEN
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = USA_joined_league
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_guaranteed_by = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				give_guarantee = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					gives_military_access_to = FROM
				}
			}
			give_military_access = FROM
		}
		add_ideas = USA_league_of_america_1
		USA = {
		add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.253
					days = 2
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = USA
				modifier = USA_joined_league
			}
			clr_country_flag = USA_sent_league_invite
			USA = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = protect
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.250.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					tag = MEX
					tag = CEN
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = YUC
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_dislikes_govt
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.251
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Remove the League idea
	id = ustates.254
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.254"}
	title = ustates.254.t
	desc = ustates.254.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = USA
			tag = WCC
			tag = CAL
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_league_of_america_1
			has_idea = USA_league_of_america_2
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = USA
			}
			is_major = yes
			has_war_with = USA
			AND = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = USA
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ustates.254.a
		clr_country_flag = USA_sent_league_invite
		clr_country_flag = USA_received_industrial_aid
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_of_america_1
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_of_america_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_of_america_2
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_of_america_2
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = USA_joined_league
		}
		USA = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = USA_joined_league
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_guaranteed_by = USA
			}
			USA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				gives_military_access_to = USA
			}
			USA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = -1
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = protect
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Change League idea
	id = ustates.255
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.255"}
	title = ustates.255.t
	desc = ustates.255.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_completed_focus = USA_defensive_navy
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USA_league_head_1
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_1
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 1
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USA_league_head_2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_2
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 9
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USA_league_head_3
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_3
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ustates.255.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_1
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 1
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_head_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_2
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 9
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_head_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_3
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_head_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USA_league_head_1
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_league_head_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USA_league_head_2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_league_head_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USA_league_head_3
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_league_head_3
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # USA is installing puppet - resist?
	id = ustates.256
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.256"}
	title = ustates.256.t
	desc = ustates.256.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.256.a #They dare!
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.257
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_of_america_1
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_of_america_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_of_america_2
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_of_america_2
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = USA_joined_league
		}
		USA = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = USA_joined_league
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_guaranteed_by = USA
			}
			USA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				gives_military_access_to = USA
			}
			USA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = -1
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = protect
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.256.b #There is nothing we can do
		add_stability = -0.20
		add_political_power = -200
	}
}

country_event = { # USA offers advisors
	id = ustates.260
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.260"}
	title = ustates.260.t
	desc = ustates.260.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FROM
			has_idea = USA_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = CAL_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = TEX_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = CSA_american_advisors_1
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_together_with = FROM
			any_enemy_country = {
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.260.a # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_offered_advisors
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = USA
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_american_advisors_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = CAL
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CAL_american_advisors_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = CSA
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CSA_american_advisors_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = TEX
				}
			}
			add_ideas = TEX_american_advisors_1
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						gives_military_access_to = FROM
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
					}
				}
				give_military_access = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = ustates.262
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.260.b # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 100
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = ustates.261
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # asking for New England Back
	id = ustates.270
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.270"}
	title = ustates.270.t
	desc = ustates.270.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Lets not risk a war.
		name = ustates.270.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = {
					exists = yes
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				end_puppet = NEE
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						exists = yes
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
				NEE = {
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = CAN
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
					remove_claim_by = CAN
				}
				FROM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.271
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall never give into yankee arrogance
		name = ustates.270.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_war_with = GER
					has_war_with = FRA
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				NEE = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.272
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England has been returned to us
	id = ustates.271
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.271"}
	title = ustates.271.t
	desc = ustates.271.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_avoided_flag
		}
		NOT = {
			NEE = {
			is_ai = no
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.271.a
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NEE }
			annex_country = {
				target = NEE
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = CAN
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			ROOT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # SPQA Election
	id = ustates.3124
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3124"}
	title = ustates.3124.t
	desc = ustates.3124.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Republican
		name = ustates.3124.a
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		OR = { 
		has_country_flag = USA_republican_convention_snell
		has_country_flag = USA_republican_convention_taber
				}
			}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.12
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Bertrand Snell
				limit = {
					OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_republican_convention_taber
					has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_dewey
					}
				}
				add_ideas = USA_Dwight_D_Eisenhower_hog_mli
				add_ideas = USA_John_Foster_Dulles_for_mli
				add_ideas = USA_Ray_Lyman_Wilbur_Sr_eco_mli
				add_ideas = USA_Fannie_Coralie_Perkins_sec_sli
			}
			if = { # John Taber
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_republican_convention_snell
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_taft
					}
				}
				add_ideas = USA_Dwight_D_Eisenhower_hog_mli 
				add_ideas = USA_John_Foster_Dulles_for_mli
				add_ideas = USA_Vannevar_Bush_eco_sli

			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.3160
				days = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.204
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.205
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = ustates.3124.b
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election

			set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Carter Glass
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_democratic_convention_glass
				}
				add_ideas = USA_Happy_Chandler_hog_sco
				add_ideas = USA_John_Foster_Dulles_for_mli
				add_ideas = USA_William_Daniel_Leahy_eco_sco
				add_ideas = USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
			}
			if = { # Sam Rayburn
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_democratic_convention_rayburn
				}

country_event = {# Trial of the US Generals
	id = ustates.3145
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3145"}
	title = ustates.3145.t
	desc = {
		text = ustates.3145.d
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_USA_military_trial
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {# Arrest the Generals
		name = ustates.3145.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 14511 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Hines
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 66 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Brooks
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 68 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Keyes
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 70 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Wainwright
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 82 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Griswold
		add_political_power = -20
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
	}
	
	option = {# Discharge them
		name = ustates.3145.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 14511 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Hines
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 66 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Brooks
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 68 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Keyes
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 70 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Wainwright
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 82 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			} #Griswold
		add_political_power = -10
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
	}
	
	option = {# Keep them!
		name = ustates.3145.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_political_power = 40
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Fifth Political System
	id = ustates.3150
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3150"}
	title = ustates.3150.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	NOT = {
		OR = {
		has_idea = USA_REP_NAZBOL
		has_idea = USA_Mckinley
		has_idea = USA_Dem_Rep
		has_idea = USA_Prog_Rep
		}
	}
	}
	
	desc = {
	text = ustates.3150.d.progs
	trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_cincinnatus_election_progressive
		}
	}
	option = { # Very Well
		name = ustates.3150.a
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_country_flag = USA_cincinnatus_election_progressive
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = USA_prog_dominance_long
			name = USA_prog_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			long_name = USA_prog_dominance_long
			name = USA_prog_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			long_name = USA_prog_dominance_long
			name = USA_prog_dominance_party }	
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			long_name = USA_prog_dominance_long
			name = USA_prog_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			long_name = USA_prog_dominance_long
			name = USA_prog_dominance_party }		
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			long_name = USA_liberal_dominance_long
			name = USA_liberal_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = USA_liberal_dominance_long
			name = USA_liberal_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			long_name = USA_liberal_dominance_long
			name = USA_liberal_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = USA_liberal_dominance_long
			name = USA_liberal_dominance_party }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			long_name = USA_liberal_dominance_long
			name = USA_liberal_dominance_party }
		set_country_flag = USA_progressive_dominance
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Results are in
	id = ustates.3198
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3198"}
	title = ustates.3198.t

	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
	has_country_flag = ACW_navy_voting_starts
	CAL = {
	exists = yes
		}
	USA = {
	exists = yes
		}
	OR = {
	AND = {
	CAL = { 
	is_ai = no
		}
	tag = CAL
	}
	AND = {
	USA = { 
	is_ai = no
		}
	tag = USA
	}
	}
	NOT = {
	OR = {
	CAL = {
	has_war_with = USA
	has_war_with = WCC
			}
	USA = {
	has_war_with = WCC
	has_war_with = CAL
			}
		}
	}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes 

	option = {
	name = ustates.3198.a
	if = {
	limit = {
	USA = {
	exists = yes
	has_global_flag = ACW_NAVY_MARSHALL_ACCEPTS_PEACE
		}
	}

	target = USA
	transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}

			}
		}
	}
	}

	if = {

	exists = yes
	has_global_flag = ACW_NAVY_MARSHALL_ACCEPTS_PEACE
		}
	}

			}

	limit = {

	exists = yes
	has_global_flag = ACW_NAVY_MARSHALL_ACCEPTS_PEACE
		}
	}

	target = CAL
	transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}

		}

# MacArthur takes over government due to inaction
country_event = {
	id = ustates.526
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.526"}
	title = ustates.526.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_macarthur_speech

	desc = {
		text = ustates.526.d.reed
		trigger = { has_idea = USA_William_Haywood_hog_syn }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.526.d.long
		trigger = { has_idea = USA_Huey_Long_hog_ade }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.526.d.oldguard
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = USA_William_Haywood_hog_syn
				has_idea = USA_Huey_Long_hog_ade
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_macarthur_coup
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = USA_paternal_autocrat_military_junta_long
				name = USA_paternal_autocrat_military_junta
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Douglas MacArthur"
				desc = "POLITICS_DOUGLAS_MACARTHUR_DESC"
				picture = "GFX_Portrait_USA_general_douglas_macarthur_animated"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = junta_subtype
				traits = { american_caesar }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.1150.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength2
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_AFP_gains_strength2
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_ODP_gains_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 3 }
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_pau
			add_ideas = USA_John_William_Davis_for_pau
			add_ideas = USA_William_Harrison_Standley_eco_pau
			add_ideas = USA_John_Edgar_Hoover_sec_pau
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.135 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.1001 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.136 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.137 days = 4 }
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.3000 days = 5 }
			LEC = {
				country_event = { id = lecyankded.8 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
			id = ustates.1281
			days = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

# PSA wants MacArthur Arrested First
country_event = {
	id = ustates.532
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.532"}
	title = ustates.532.t
	desc = ustates.532.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAL_golden_gate_crowd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = CAL }
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.532.a #For the good of America, let it be done
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_sco
				has_idea = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_pau
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CAL = { has_country_flag = CAL_miss_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				CAL = { has_country_flag = CAL_rocky_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur }
			set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_garner
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 56 }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 56 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.10
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		CAL = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.534 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.532.b #MacArthur is a hero - refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
					has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_considering_reunion
		add_political_power = 50
		CAL = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.533 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

				limit = { has_unit_leader = 56 }

				limit = { has_id = 56 }

			}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.998.a

			factor = 5
		}

		}
